***хмуриться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хмуриться.html>хму́риться</a> (7746)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмурить.html>хму́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xmúritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмуриться.html>хму́риться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xmúritʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нахмуриться.html>нахму́риться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to frown</li>
<li>to gloom, to lour (of rain clouds)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмурить.html>хму́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xmúritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">

***хныкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хныкать.html>хны́кать</a> (22610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoetic in origin. Compare dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмыкать.html>хмы́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xmýkatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whine, to whimper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">хни́кати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xnýkaty</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whine, to whimper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and similar verbs in other languages, such as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">kníkati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whine, to squeal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">kničeti</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">kňučeti</i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">knychać</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whine, to squeal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">šnukstêt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sob, to whine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnucken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sigh, to sob, to whimper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хныкать.html>хны́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xnýkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to whine, to whimper</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to complain tearfully, to sob</li></ol>

***ход.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a> (501)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ходъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xodъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sod-</i>, whence Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὁδός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hodós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">threshold; road, path, journey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and thereby English suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ode</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хо́да</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>motion, movement, travel, progress, locomotion, headway</li>
<li>course, path, way, run</li>
<li>speed, rate, gait, pace</li>
<li>stroke <i>(of a piston)</i></li>
<li>functioning, working, process, action</li>
<li>gear, thread, pitch</li>
<li>shape, trend, dependence <i>(of a curve)</i></li>
<li>range <i>(of a magnet)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ходы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ходо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>entrance, entry</li>
<li>passage</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ходы́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ходо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> move, turn, lead</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хода́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ходо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>axle with wheels</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходатайствовать.html>хода́тайствовать</a> (23335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходатайство.html>хода́тайство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodátajstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходатайствовать.html>хода́тайствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xodátajstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">похода́тайствовать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to solicit <i>(for)</i>, to apply <i>(for)</i>, to intercede <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходатайствовать.html>хода́тайствовать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судья.html>су́дьями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodátajstvovatʹ</b> péred súdʹjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to solicit the judges</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> (256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoditi</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходя́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hodja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> , <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">hodati</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">chodit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сходить.html>сходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go, to walk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пешком.html>пешко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> peškóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to walk, to go on foot, to hike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокруг.html>вокру́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:около.html>о́коло</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> vokrúg da ókolo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat around the bush</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to walk around and near</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>хо́дят</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слу́хи</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>хо́дит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xódjat</b> slúxi; <b>xódit</b> slux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is rumored</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> го́голем</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> gógolem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strut</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>миру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> pó miru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beg</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходун.html>ходуно́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xodunóm <b>xodítʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shake, to tremble, to rock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:босиком.html>босико́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> bosikóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go barefoot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведка.html>разве́дку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> v razvédku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go on reconnaissance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> вперева́лку/<a href = vnd.unilang:вразвалку.html>вразва́лку</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:вразвалочку.html>вразва́лочку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> vpereválku/vrazválku/vrazváločku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to waddle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> na lýžax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ski</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> na oxótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go shooting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:процедура.html>процеду́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> na procedúry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take treatment</span></div></dd>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шуба.html>шу́бе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> v šúbe</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to wear a</b> winter coat</span></div></dd>

<li>to go (to), to attend, to visit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> v škólu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to school, to attend school</span></div></dd>

<li>to run <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of trains, ships, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>паруса́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodítʹ</b> pod parusámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sail</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>хо́дят</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:всюду.html>всю́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éti dénʹgi <b>xódjat</b> vsjúdu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this currency is good anywhere</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is in the class of Russian abstract verbs. Its counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pojtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.
</p>

***ходовой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходово́й</a> (17088)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xodovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> motion, run
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:винт.html>винт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodovój</b> vint</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>guide/lead</b> screw</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>коне́ц</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodovój</b> konéc</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>running</b> end <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a knot</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodovája</b> častʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>running</b> gear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходовы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́чества</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodovýje</b> káčestva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">road performance <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a car</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>riding/running</b> characteristics</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходовы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:испытание.html>испыта́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodovýje</b> ispytánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>performance/running</b> trials</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>salable, marketable, best-selling, highly demanded <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of goods</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>common, commonly used <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a word</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходовой.html>ходово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выражение.html>выраже́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodovóje</b> vyražénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>current/common</b> expression/phrase; byword, catchword</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xodьba</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoditi</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьba</i>. ***ходячий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чий</a> (15344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jáčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходя́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodjáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xodjáčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>walking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčij</b> bolʹnój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">walking patient</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>current
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:истина.html>и́стина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčaja</b> ístina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">truism</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мнение.html>мне́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčeje</b> mnénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">current/common opinion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фраза.html>фра́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčaja</b> fráza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">current phrase; catchword; byword</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мощь.html>мо́щи</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">ironic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčije</b> móšči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a walking skeleton</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> walking, personified, incarnate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доказательство.html>доказа́тельство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčeje</b> dokazátelʹstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">walking proof</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:энциклопедия.html>энциклопе́дия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčaja</b> enciklopédija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">walking encyclopaedia</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ходячий.html>ходя́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:добродетель.html>доброде́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xodjáčaja</b> dobrodételʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">virtue incarnate</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***хозяин.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ин</a> (370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">хозя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xozja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chuvash_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chuvash language">Chuvash</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="cv">хуҫа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">huśa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خواجه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xâje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">hoca</i>, Slavic: <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">хазя́їн</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xazjájin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">хадзя́ін</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xadzjáin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ин</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xozjáin</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ина</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ева</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>хозя́йка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>owner, proprietor</li>
<li>landlord, housekeeper</li>
<li>boss, master, chief, principal, manager, employer, hirer</li>
<li>man, husband</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> host, master</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> host</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>хозя́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xozjájka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>хозя́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>хозя́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйка.html>хозя́ек</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>owner, proprietor <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">female</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>hostess</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wife</li></ol>

***хозяйничать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйничать.html>хозя́йничать</a> (15798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ин</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xozjáin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ничать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ničatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйничать.html>хозя́йничать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xozjájničatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to keep house, to manage a household</li>
<li>to do household chores
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйничать.html>хозя́йничает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná sejčás <b>xozjájničajet</b> na kúxne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she is bustling about in the kitchen</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to boss it, to play the master, to lord it</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хозя́й-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xozjáj-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйский.html>хозя́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xozjájskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>owner, landlord, master, boss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйский.html>хозя́йским</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>гла́зом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xozjájskim</b> glázom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with a thrifty master's eye</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйский.html>хозя́йскую</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:забота.html>забо́ту</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">projavítʹ <b>xozjájskuju</b> zabótu (o)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">take a proprietary interest (in)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйский.html>хозя́йское</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délo <b>xozjájskoje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is for you to decide; it is up to you; you are your own master</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lordly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйский.html>хозя́йским</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>то́ном</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">govorítʹ <b>xozjájskim</b> tónom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">speak in a lordly tone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> host</li></ol>

***хозяйственник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственник.html>хозя́йственник</a> (18912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственный.html>хозя́йственный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xozjájstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственник.html>хозя́йственник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xozjájstvennik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственник.html>хозя́йственника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственник.html>хозя́йственники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственник.html>хозя́йственников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хозя́йственница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>business manager</li>
<li>an economic/thrifty man</li>
<li>handyman, someone who is good with his hands and managing a property</li></ol>
